import json
from datetime import date, timedelta

# Real server date
today = date(2026, 5, 24)
week_start = date(2026, 5, 18)  # Saturday of current week (18 = Saturday)

with open('/workspace/app-bqosbzxnngu9/src/data/sales.json') as f:
    sales = json.load(f)

# Rebuild dates: spread 15 records across this week + this month
# Today (May 24): 3 records, This week (May 18-24): 5 records, This month (May 1-24): all 15
new_dates = [
    f"{today}T08:30:00",        # today
    f"{today}T11:00:00",        # today
    f"{today}T15:45:00",        # today
    "2026-05-23T09:00:00",      # yesterday (fri)
    "2026-05-23T14:00:00",      # yesterday (fri)
    "2026-05-22T10:30:00",      # this week
    "2026-05-21T13:00:00",      # this week
    "2026-05-20T09:00:00",      # this week
    "2026-05-18T11:00:00",      # this week (sat)
    "2026-05-17T10:00:00",      # last week
    "2026-05-15T09:30:00",      # last week
    "2026-05-13T14:00:00",      # mid month
    "2026-05-10T11:00:00",      # mid month
    "2026-05-05T09:00:00",      # early month
    "2026-05-01T08:00:00",      # month start
]

for i, s in enumerate(sales):
    s['date'] = new_dates[i]

with open('/workspace/app-bqosbzxnngu9/src/data/sales.json', 'w') as f:
    json.dump(sales, f, indent=2)

# Verify
today_str = str(today)
week_start_str = "2026-05-18"
month_start_str = "2026-05-01"

today_count  = sum(1 for s in sales if s['date'][:10] == today_str)
week_count   = sum(1 for s in sales if week_start_str <= s['date'][:10] <= today_str)
month_count  = sum(1 for s in sales if month_start_str <= s['date'][:10] <= today_str)

print(f"Today ({today_str}):        {today_count} records")
print(f"This week ({week_start_str}–{today_str}): {week_count} records")
print(f"This month ({month_start_str}–{today_str}): {month_count} records")

import os, re

BAD = re.compile(r'(?<![`\w])\$\{[\w.?()]+\}|>\s*\$\{|>\s*؋\{|`\$\$\{|`؋\$\{')
SKIP = {'fmtCurrency', '//', 'padStart', 'generateId', 'TXN-', 'PUR-', 'EXP-',
        'STR-', 'className', 'toFixed(1)', "t('signIn')", 'import ', "`."}

found = []
for root, _, files in os.walk('/workspace/app-bqosbzxnngu9/src'):
    for fname in files:
        if not fname.endswith(('.jsx', '.tsx', '.js', '.ts')): continue
        fpath = os.path.join(root, fname)
        with open(fpath) as f:
            for i, line in enumerate(f, 1):
                if BAD.search(line) and not any(s in line for s in SKIP):
                    found.append(f"{fpath.replace('/workspace/app-bqosbzxnngu9/src/','src/')}:{i}: {line.rstrip()}")

if found:
    print("REMAINING RAW CURRENCY:")
    for l in found: print(' ', l)
else:
    print("✓ No raw currency symbols found")

  const {data: customers = []} = useQuery({queryKey: ['customers'],
    queryFn: customersApi.getAll});

  const periodLabel = {daily_sales: t('dailySales'),

    doc.text(periodLabel[reportType], 14, 20);
    doc.setFontSize(10);
    doc.text(`${t('period')}: ${dateFrom} ${t('to')} ${dateTo}`, 14, 30);

import {useReactToPrint} from 'react-to-print';

import {salesApi, purchasesApi, expensesApi, lossesApi, tanksApi, fuelTypesApi, customersApi} from '@/services/api';

import AppLayout from '@/components/layouts/AppLayout'; import {useI18n, fmtCurrency} from '@/lib/i18n'; import {Button} from '@/components/ui/button'; import {Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle} from '@/components/ui/card'; import {Input} from '@/components/ui/input'; import {Select, SelectContent, SelectItem, SelectTrigger, SelectValue} from '@/components/ui/select';

// Safely extract date-only portion (handles ISO strings and plain dates) function toDateStr(d) { if (!d) return ''; return String(d).substring(0, 10); }

function inRange(d, start, end) { const ds = toDateStr(d); return ds >= start && ds <= end; }

export default function ReportsPage() { const today = format(new Date(), 'yyyy-MM-dd'); const [reportType, setReportType] = useState('daily_sales'); const {t, lang} = useI18n();

// Each report type carries its own sensible default date range const defaultRanges = { daily_sales: {from: today, to: today}, weekly_sales: {from: format(startOfWeek(new Date(), {weekStartsOn: 6}), 'yyyy-MM-dd'), to: today}, monthly_sales: {from: format(startOfMonth(new Date()), 'yyyy-MM-dd'), to: format(endOfMonth(new Date()), 'yyyy-MM-dd')}, fuel_stock: {from: format(startOfMonth(new Date()), 'yyyy-MM-dd'), to: today}, profit: {from: format(startOfMonth(new Date()), 'yyyy-MM-dd'), to: today}, loss: {from: format(startOfMonth(new Date()), 'yyyy-MM-dd'), to: today}, expense: {from: format(startOfMonth(new Date()), 'yyyy-MM-dd'), to: today}, credit: {from: format(startOfMonth(new Date()), 'yyyy-MM-dd'), to: today}, daily_summary: {from: today, to: today}, monthly_summary: {from: format(startOfMonth(new Date()), 'yyyy-MM-dd'), to: format(endOfMonth(new Date()), 'yyyy-MM-dd')}, };

const [dateFrom, setDateFrom] = useState(defaultRanges.daily_sales.from); const [dateTo, setDateTo] = useState(defaultRanges.daily_sales.to); const printRef = useRef(null);

// When report type changes, update date range to the sensible default const handleReportTypeChange = (v) => { setReportType(v); const range = defaultRanges[v]; if (range) { setDateFrom(range.from); setDateTo(range.to); } };

const { data: sales = []} = useQuery({queryKey: ['sales'], queryFn: salesApi.getAll}); const {data: purchases = []} = useQuery({queryKey: ['purchases'], queryFn: purchasesApi.getAll}); const {data: expenses = []} = useQuery({queryKey: ['expenses'], queryFn: expensesApi.getAll}); const {data: losses = []} = useQuery({queryKey: ['losses'], queryFn: lossesApi.getAll}); const {data: tanks = []} = useQuery({queryKey: ['tanks'], queryFn: tanksApi.getAll}); const {data: fuelTypes = []} = useQuery({queryKey: ['fuelTypes'], queryFn: fuelTypesApi.getAll}); const {data: customers = []} = useQuery({queryKey: ['customers'], queryFn: customersApi.getAll});

const periodLabel = { daily_sales: t('dailySales'), weekly_sales: t('weeklySales'), monthly_sales: t('monthlySales'), fuel_stock: t('fuelStockReport'), profit: t('profitReport'), loss: t('lossReport'), expense: t('expenseReport'), credit: t('creditReport'), daily_summary: t('dailySummary'), monthly_summary: t('monthlySummary'), };

const handlePrint = useReactToPrint({contentRef: printRef});

const handlePDF = () => { const reportData = getReportData(); if (!reportData) return; const {columns, rows, summary} = reportData; const doc = new jsPDF(); doc.setFontSize(16); doc.text(periodLabel[reportType] ?? reportType, 14, 20); doc.setFontSize(10); doc.text(${t('period')}: ${dateFrom} ${t('to')} ${dateTo}, 14, 30); doc.text(${t('generated')}: ${format(new Date(), 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm')}, 14, 37); let startY = 48; if (summary.length > 0) { doc.setFontSize(11); doc.text(t('metric'), 14, 50); summary.forEach((s, i) => { doc.setFontSize(9); doc.text(${s.label}: ${s.value}, 14, 58 + i * 7); }); startY = 58 + summary.length * 7 + 8; } autoTable(doc, { head: [columns], body: rows, startY, styles: {fontSize: 8}, }); doc.save(${reportType}-${dateFrom}.pdf); };

// Filter helpers — safe against ISO timestamps and plain date strings const filteredSales = sales.filter((s) => inRange(s.date, dateFrom, dateTo)); const filteredPurchases = purchases.filter((p) => inRange(p.date, dateFrom, dateTo)); const filteredExpenses = expenses.filter((e) => inRange(e.date, dateFrom, dateTo)); const filteredLosses = losses.filter((l) => inRange(l.date, dateFrom, dateTo));

function getReportData() { switch (reportType) { case 'daily_sales': case 'weekly_sales': case 'monthly_sales': { const totalRev = filteredSales.reduce((a, s) => a + (s.totalAmount ?? 0), 0); const totalL = filteredSales.reduce((a, s) => a + (s.liters ?? 0), 0); return { columns: [t('transactionId'), t('customer'), t('fuel'), t('liters'), t('pricePerLiter'), t('total'), t('method'), t('date')], rows: filteredSales.map((s) => [ s.transactionId ?? '', s.customerName ?? '-', fuelTypes.find((f) => f.id === s.fuelTypeId)?.name ?? '-', ${s.liters ?? 0}L, fmtCurrency(s.pricePerLiter ?? 0, lang, 3), fmtCurrency(s.totalAmount ?? 0, lang), s.paymentMethod ?? '', toDateStr(s.date), ]), summary: [ {label: t('totalTransactions'), value: String(filteredSales.length)}, {label: t('totalRevenue'), value: fmtCurrency(totalRev, lang)}, {label: t('totalLitersSold'), value: ${totalL}L}, ], }; } case 'fuel_stock': return { columns: [t('name'), t('fuel'), t('capacityL'), t('currentStockL'), t('minLevelL'), t('usage'), t('status')], rows: tanks.map((tank) => { const ft = fuelTypes.find((f) => f.id === tank.fuelTypeId); const usagePct = tank.capacity > 0 ? Math.round((tank.currentStock / tank.capacity) * 100) : 0; return [ tank.name ?? '', ft?.name ?? '-', ${tank.capacity ?? 0}L, ${tank.currentStock ?? 0}L, ${tank.minimumLevel ?? 0}L, ${usagePct}%, t(tank.status) || tank.status, ]; }), summary: [ {label: t('totalTanks'), value: String(tanks.length)}, {label: t('totalStock'), value: ${tanks.reduce((a, tk) => a + (tk.currentStock ?? 0), 0).toLocaleString()}L}, ], }; case 'profit': { const rev = filteredSales.reduce((a, s) => a + (s.totalAmount ?? 0), 0); const cost = filteredPurchases.reduce((a, p) => a + (p.totalAmount ?? 0), 0); const exp = filteredExpenses.reduce((a, e) => a + (e.amount ?? 0), 0); const net = rev - cost - exp; return { columns: [t('period'), t('revenue'), t('fuelCost'), t('expenses'), t('netProfit')], rows: [[ ${dateFrom} → ${dateTo}, fmtCurrency(rev, lang), fmtCurrency(cost, lang), fmtCurrency(exp, lang), fmtCurrency(net, lang), ]], summary: [ {label: t('revenue'), value: fmtCurrency(rev, lang)}, {label: t('fuelCost'), value: fmtCurrency(cost, lang)}, {label: t('expenses'), value: fmtCurrency(exp, lang)}, {label: t('netProfit'), value: fmtCurrency(net, lang)}, ], }; } case 'loss': return { columns: [t('lossId'), t('type'), t('amount'), t('date'), t('description')], rows: filteredLosses.map((l) => [ l.lossId ?? '', l.lossType ?? '', fmtCurrency(l.amount ?? 0, lang), toDateStr(l.date), l.description ?? '', ]), summary: [ {label: t('totalLosses'), value: fmtCurrency(filteredLosses.reduce((a, l) => a + (l.amount ?? 0), 0), lang)}, ], }; case 'expense': return { columns: [t('expenseId'), t('type'), t('amount'), t('date'), t('description')], rows: filteredExpenses.map((e) => [ e.expenseId ?? '', e.type ?? '', fmtCurrency(e.amount ?? 0, lang), toDateStr(e.date), e.description ?? '', ]), summary: [ {label: t('totalExpenses'), value: fmtCurrency(filteredExpenses.reduce((a, e) => a + (e.amount ?? 0), 0), lang)}, ], }; case 'credit': { const creditCusts = customers.filter((c) => c.type === 'credit'); return { columns: [t('customerId'), t('name'), t('phone'), t('creditBalance'), t('creditLimit'), t('status')], rows: creditCusts.map((c) => [ c.customerId ?? '', c.fullName ?? '', c.phone ?? '', fmtCurrency(c.creditBalance ?? 0, lang), fmtCurrency(c.creditLimit ?? 0, lang), t(c.status) || c.status, ]), summary: [ {label: t('totalCreditCustomers'), value: String(creditCusts.length)}, {label: t('totalOutstanding'), value: fmtCurrency(creditCusts.reduce((a, c) => a + (c.creditBalance ?? 0), 0), lang)}, ], }; } case 'daily_summary': case 'monthly_summary': { const rev = filteredSales.reduce((a, s) => a + (s.totalAmount ?? 0), 0); const exp = filteredExpenses.reduce((a, e) => a + (e.amount ?? 0), 0); const cost = filteredPurchases.reduce((a, p) => a + (p.totalAmount ?? 0), 0); const totalL = filteredSales.reduce((a, s) => a + (s.liters ?? 0), 0); return { columns: [t('metric'), t('value')], rows: [ [t('totalSalesLabel'), fmtCurrency(rev, lang)], [t('totalFuelCost'), fmtCurrency(cost, lang)], [t('totalExpenses'), fmtCurrency(exp, lang)], [t('netProfit'), fmtCurrency(rev - cost - exp, lang)], [t('totalTransactions'), String(filteredSales.length)], [t('totalLitersSold'), ${totalL}L], ], summary: [ {label: t('totalRevenue'), value: fmtCurrency(rev, lang)}, {label: t('netProfit'), value: fmtCurrency(rev - cost - exp, lang)}, {label: t('totalTransactions'), value: String(filteredSales.length)}, ], }; } default: return {columns: [], rows: [], summary: []}; } }

const reportData = getReportData(); const {columns, rows, summary} = reportData ?? {columns: [], rows: [], summary: []};

import {useRef, useState} from 'react';
import {useQuery} from '@tanstack/react-query';
import {FiPrinter, FiDownload, FiFileText} from 'react-icons/fi';
import {format, startOfMonth, endOfMonth, startOfWeek} from 'date-fns';
import jsPDF from 'jspdf';
import autoTable from 'jspdf-autotable';
import {useReactToPrint} from 'react-to-print';
import {salesApi, purchasesApi, expensesApi, lossesApi, tanksApi, fuelTypesApi, customersApi} from '@/services/api';
import AppLayout from '@/components/layouts/AppLayout';
import {useI18n, fmtCurrency} from '@/lib/i18n';
import {Button} from '@/components/ui/button';
import {Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle} from '@/components/ui/card';
import {Input} from '@/components/ui/input';
import {Select, SelectContent, SelectItem, SelectTrigger, SelectValue} from '@/components/ui/select';

// Safely extract date-only portion (handles ISO timestamps and plain YYYY-MM-DD)
function toDateStr(d) { return d ? String(d).substring(0, 10) : ''; }
function inRange(d, start, end) { const ds = toDateStr(d); return ds >= start && ds <= end; }

export default function ReportsPage() {
  const today = format(new Date(), 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  const {t, lang} = useI18n();

  const defaultRanges = {
    daily_sales:     {from: today, to: today},
    weekly_sales:    {from: format(startOfWeek(new Date(), {weekStartsOn: 6}), 'yyyy-MM-dd'), to: today},
    monthly_sales:   {from: format(startOfMonth(new Date()), 'yyyy-MM-dd'), to: format(endOfMonth(new Date()), 'yyyy-MM-dd')},
    fuel_stock:      {from: format(startOfMonth(new Date()), 'yyyy-MM-dd'), to: today},
    profit:          {from: format(startOfMonth(new Date()), 'yyyy-MM-dd'), to: today},
    loss:            {from: format(startOfMonth(new Date()), 'yyyy-MM-dd'), to: today},
    expense:         {from: format(startOfMonth(new Date()), 'yyyy-MM-dd'), to: today},
    credit:          {from: format(startOfMonth(new Date()), 'yyyy-MM-dd'), to: today},
    daily_summary:   {from: today, to: today},
    monthly_summary: {from: format(startOfMonth(new Date()), 'yyyy-MM-dd'), to: format(endOfMonth(new Date()), 'yyyy-MM-dd')},
  };

  const [reportType, setReportType] = useState('daily_sales');
  const [dateFrom, setDateFrom] = useState(defaultRanges.daily_sales.from);
  const [dateTo, setDateTo]     = useState(defaultRanges.daily_sales.to);
  const printRef = useRef(null);

  const handleReportTypeChange = (v) => {
    setReportType(v);
    const r = defaultRanges[v];
    if (r) { setDateFrom(r.from); setDateTo(r.to); }
  };

  const {data: sales = []}     = useQuery({queryKey: ['sales'],     queryFn: salesApi.getAll});
  const {data: purchases = []} = useQuery({queryKey: ['purchases'], queryFn: purchasesApi.getAll});
  const {data: expenses = []}  = useQuery({queryKey: ['expenses'],  queryFn: expensesApi.getAll});
  const {data: losses = []}    = useQuery({queryKey: ['losses'],    queryFn: lossesApi.getAll});
  const {data: tanks = []}     = useQuery({queryKey: ['tanks'],     queryFn: tanksApi.getAll});
  const {data: fuelTypes = []} = useQuery({queryKey: ['fuelTypes'], queryFn: fuelTypesApi.getAll});
  const {data: customers = []} = useQuery({queryKey: ['customers'], queryFn: customersApi.getAll});

  const periodLabel = {
    daily_sales:     t('dailySales'),
    weekly_sales:    t('weeklySales'),
    monthly_sales:   t('monthlySales'),
    fuel_stock:      t('fuelStockReport'),
    profit:          t('profitReport'),
    loss:            t('lossReport'),
    expense:         t('expenseReport'),
    credit:          t('creditReport'),
    daily_summary:   t('dailySummary'),
    monthly_summary: t('monthlySummary'),
  };

  const handlePrint = useReactToPrint({contentRef: printRef});

  const handlePDF = () => {
    const rd = getReportData();
    if (!rd) return;
    const {columns, rows, summary} = rd;
    const doc = new jsPDF();
    doc.setFontSize(16);
    doc.text(periodLabel[reportType] ?? reportType, 14, 20);
    doc.setFontSize(10);
    doc.text(`${t('period')}: ${dateFrom} ${t('to')} ${dateTo}`, 14, 30);
    doc.text(`${t('generated')}: ${format(new Date(), 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm')}`, 14, 37);
    let startY = 48;
    if (summary.length > 0) {
      doc.setFontSize(11);
      doc.text(t('metric'), 14, 50);
      summary.forEach((s, i) => { doc.setFontSize(9); doc.text(`${s.label}: ${s.value}`, 14, 58 + i * 7); });
      startY = 58 + summary.length * 7 + 8;
    }
    autoTable(doc, {head: [columns], body: rows, startY, styles: {fontSize: 8}});
    doc.save(`${reportType}-${dateFrom}.pdf`);
  };

  const filteredSales     = sales.filter((s) => inRange(s.date, dateFrom, dateTo));
  const filteredPurchases = purchases.filter((p) => inRange(p.date, dateFrom, dateTo));
  const filteredExpenses  = expenses.filter((e) => inRange(e.date, dateFrom, dateTo));
  const filteredLosses    = losses.filter((l) => inRange(l.date, dateFrom, dateTo));

  function getReportData() {
    switch (reportType) {
      case 'daily_sales':
      case 'weekly_sales':
      case 'monthly_sales': {
        const totalRev = filteredSales.reduce((a, s) => a + (s.totalAmount ?? 0), 0);
        const totalL   = filteredSales.reduce((a, s) => a + (s.liters ?? 0), 0);
        return {
          columns: [t('transactionId'), t('customer'), t('fuel'), t('liters'), t('pricePerLiter'), t('total'), t('method'), t('date')],
          rows: filteredSales.map((s) => [
            s.transactionId ?? '',
            s.customerName ?? '-',
            fuelTypes.find((f) => f.id === s.fuelTypeId)?.name ?? '-',
            `${s.liters ?? 0}L`,
            fmtCurrency(s.pricePerLiter ?? 0, lang, 3),
            fmtCurrency(s.totalAmount ?? 0, lang),
            s.paymentMethod ?? '',
            toDateStr(s.date),
          ]),
          summary: [
            {label: t('totalTransactions'), value: String(filteredSales.length)},
            {label: t('totalRevenue'),      value: fmtCurrency(totalRev, lang)},
            {label: t('totalLitersSold'),   value: `${totalL}L`},
          ],
        };
      }
      case 'fuel_stock':
        return {
          columns: [t('name'), t('fuel'), t('capacityL'), t('currentStockL'), t('minLevelL'), t('usage'), t('status')],
          rows: tanks.map((tank) => {
            const ft = fuelTypes.find((f) => f.id === tank.fuelTypeId);
            const pct = tank.capacity > 0 ? Math.round((tank.currentStock / tank.capacity) * 100) : 0;
            return [tank.name ?? '', ft?.name ?? '-', `${tank.capacity ?? 0}L`, `${tank.currentStock ?? 0}L`, `${tank.minimumLevel ?? 0}L`, `${pct}%`, t(tank.status) || tank.status];
          }),
          summary: [
            {label: t('totalTanks'),  value: String(tanks.length)},
            {label: t('totalStock'),  value: `${tanks.reduce((a, tk) => a + (tk.currentStock ?? 0), 0).toLocaleString()}L`},
          ],
        };
      case 'profit': {
        const rev  = filteredSales.reduce((a, s) => a + (s.totalAmount ?? 0), 0);
        const cost = filteredPurchases.reduce((a, p) => a + (p.totalAmount ?? 0), 0);
        const exp  = filteredExpenses.reduce((a, e) => a + (e.amount ?? 0), 0);
        const net  = rev - cost - exp;
        return {
          columns: [t('period'), t('revenue'), t('fuelCost'), t('expenses'), t('netProfit')],
          rows: [[`${dateFrom} → ${dateTo}`, fmtCurrency(rev, lang), fmtCurrency(cost, lang), fmtCurrency(exp, lang), fmtCurrency(net, lang)]],
          summary: [
            {label: t('revenue'),   value: fmtCurrency(rev, lang)},
            {label: t('fuelCost'),  value: fmtCurrency(cost, lang)},
            {label: t('expenses'),  value: fmtCurrency(exp, lang)},
            {label: t('netProfit'), value: fmtCurrency(net, lang)},
          ],
        };
      }
      case 'loss':
        return {
          columns: [t('lossId'), t('type'), t('amount'), t('date'), t('description')],
          rows: filteredLosses.map((l) => [l.lossId ?? '', l.lossType ?? '', fmtCurrency(l.amount ?? 0, lang), toDateStr(l.date), l.description ?? '']),
          summary: [{label: t('totalLosses'), value: fmtCurrency(filteredLosses.reduce((a, l) => a + (l.amount ?? 0), 0), lang)}],
        };
      case 'expense':
        return {
          columns: [t('expenseId'), t('type'), t('amount'), t('date'), t('description')],
          rows: filteredExpenses.map((e) => [e.expenseId ?? '', e.type ?? '', fmtCurrency(e.amount ?? 0, lang), toDateStr(e.date), e.description ?? '']),
          summary: [{label: t('totalExpenses'), value: fmtCurrency(filteredExpenses.reduce((a, e) => a + (e.amount ?? 0), 0), lang)}],
        };
      case 'credit': {
        const creditCusts = customers.filter((c) => c.type === 'credit');
        return {
          columns: [t('customerId'), t('name'), t('phone'), t('creditBalance'), t('creditLimit'), t('status')],
          rows: creditCusts.map((c) => [c.customerId ?? '', c.fullName ?? '', c.phone ?? '', fmtCurrency(c.creditBalance ?? 0, lang), fmtCurrency(c.creditLimit ?? 0, lang), t(c.status) || c.status]),
          summary: [
            {label: t('totalCreditCustomers'), value: String(creditCusts.length)},
            {label: t('totalOutstanding'),     value: fmtCurrency(creditCusts.reduce((a, c) => a + (c.creditBalance ?? 0), 0), lang)},
          ],
        };
      }
      case 'daily_summary':
      case 'monthly_summary': {
        const rev    = filteredSales.reduce((a, s) => a + (s.totalAmount ?? 0), 0);
        const exp    = filteredExpenses.reduce((a, e) => a + (e.amount ?? 0), 0);
        const cost   = filteredPurchases.reduce((a, p) => a + (p.totalAmount ?? 0), 0);
        const totalL = filteredSales.reduce((a, s) => a + (s.liters ?? 0), 0);
        return {
          columns: [t('metric'), t('value')],
          rows: [
            [t('totalSalesLabel'),   fmtCurrency(rev, lang)],
            [t('totalFuelCost'),     fmtCurrency(cost, lang)],
            [t('totalExpenses'),     fmtCurrency(exp, lang)],
            [t('netProfit'),         fmtCurrency(rev - cost - exp, lang)],
            [t('totalTransactions'), String(filteredSales.length)],
            [t('totalLitersSold'),   `${totalL}L`],
          ],
          summary: [
            {label: t('totalRevenue'), value: fmtCurrency(rev, lang)},
            {label: t('netProfit'),    value: fmtCurrency(rev - cost - exp, lang)},
            {label: t('totalTransactions'), value: String(filteredSales.length)},
          ],
        };
      }
      default:
        return {columns: [], rows: [], summary: []};
    }
  }

  const {columns, rows, summary} = getReportData();

  return (
    <AppLayout title={t('reports')}>
      <div className="space-y-6">
        {/* Controls */}
        <Card>
          <CardContent className="p-4">
            <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-3">
              <Select value={reportType} onValueChange={handleReportTypeChange}>
                <SelectTrigger className="h-9 w-52">
                  <SelectValue />
                </SelectTrigger>
                <SelectContent>
                  {Object.keys(periodLabel).map((k) => (
                    <SelectItem key={k} value={k}>{periodLabel[k]}</SelectItem>
                  ))}
                </SelectContent>
              </Select>
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                <Input type="date" value={dateFrom} onChange={(e) => setDateFrom(e.target.value)} className="h-9 w-36" />
                <span className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">{t('to')}</span>
                <Input type="date" value={dateTo} onChange={(e) => setDateTo(e.target.value)} className="h-9 w-36" />
              </div>
              <div className="ml-auto flex items-center gap-2">
                <Button variant="outline" size="sm" onClick={handlePrint}>
                  <FiPrinter className="mr-1 h-4 w-4" /> {t('print')}
                </Button>
                <Button size="sm" onClick={handlePDF}>
                  <FiDownload className="mr-1 h-4 w-4" /> {t('exportPDF')}
                </Button>
              </div>
            </div>
          </CardContent>
        </Card>

        {/* Report Preview */}
        <div ref={printRef} className="print:p-8">
          <Card>
            <CardHeader>
              <div className="flex flex-wrap items-start justify-between gap-3">
                <div>
                  <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2 text-balance text-lg">
                    <FiFileText className="h-5 w-5 text-primary" />
                    {periodLabel[reportType]}
                  </CardTitle>
                  <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                    {t('period')}: {dateFrom} {t('to')} {dateTo}
                  </p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                    {t('generated')}: {format(new Date(), 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm')}
                  </p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </CardHeader>
            <CardContent className="p-6">
              {/* Summary KPI cards */}
              {summary.length > 0 && (
                <div className="mb-6 grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 md:grid-cols-4">
                  {summary.map((s) => (
                    <div key={s.label} className="rounded-lg bg-muted p-3">
                      <p className="text-pretty text-xs text-muted-foreground">{s.label}</p>
                      <p className="mt-0.5 text-lg font-bold text-foreground">{s.value}</p>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              )}

              {/* Data table */}
              <div className="overflow-x-auto">
                <table className="w-full whitespace-nowrap">
                  <thead>
                    <tr className="border-b border-border">
                      {columns.map((col) => (
                        <th key={col} className="py-2 pr-4 text-left text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground">
                          {col}
                        </th>
                      ))}
                    </tr>
                  </thead>
                  <tbody>
                    {rows.map((row, i) => (
                      // eslint-disable-next-line react/no-array-index-key
                      <tr key={i} className="border-b border-border transition-colors last:border-0 hover:bg-muted/30">
                        {row.map((cell, j) => (
                          // eslint-disable-next-line react/no-array-index-key
                          <td key={j} className="py-2 pr-4 text-sm">{cell}</td>
                        ))}
                      </tr>
                    ))}
                    {rows.length === 0 && (
                      <tr>
                        <td colSpan={columns.length} className="py-8 text-center text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                          {t('noData')}
                        </td>
                      </tr>
                    )}
                  </tbody>
                  {rows.length > 0 && (
                    <tfoot>
                      <tr className="border-t-2 border-border">
                        <td colSpan={columns.length} className="py-2 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                          {t('records')}: {rows.length}
                        </td>
                      </tr>
                    </tfoot>
                  )}
                </table>
              </div>

              {/* Signature section (print only) */}
              <div className="mt-16 hidden items-end justify-between border-t border-border pt-8 print:flex">

import re

# ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# DashboardPage – replace all ؋ and chart formatter
# ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

with open(fpath) as f: c = f.read()

# value={`؋${XXX.toFixed(N)}`}  →  value={fmtCurrency(XXX, lang)}
c = re.sub(r'value=\{`؋\$\{(.*?)\.toFixed\(\d+\)\}`\}', 
           lambda m: f'value={{fmtCurrency({m.group(1)}, lang)}}', c)

# value={`؋${XXX.toLocaleString(...)}`}
c = re.sub(r'value=\{`؋\$\{(.*?)\.toLocaleString\([^)]*\)\}`\}',
           lambda m: f'value={{fmtCurrency({m.group(1)}, lang)}}', c)

# chart formatter: [(v) => [`؋${v.toFixed(2)}`, '']]
c = c.replace("formatter={(v) => [`؋${v.toFixed(2)}`, '']}",
              "formatter={(v) => [fmtCurrency(v, lang), '']}")

# Inline JSX: ؋{sale.totalAmount.toFixed(2)}
c = re.sub(r'؋\{([\w.]+)\.toFixed\(\d+\)\}',
           lambda m: f'{{fmtCurrency({m.group(1)}, lang)}}', c)

# Make sure fmtCurrency is imported
if "fmtCurrency" not in c:
    c = c.replace("import {useI18n}", "import {useI18n, fmtCurrency}")

with open(fpath, 'w') as f: f.write(c)

# ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# Helper: replace `$${expr.toFixed(N)}` and `${expr.toFixed(N)}` JSX patterns
# ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
def fix_currency(c, lang_var='lang'):
    # Template literal backtick patterns inside JSX: `$${x.toFixed(2)}`
    c = re.sub(r'`\$\$\{([\w.()\[\]'"'"'? ]+)\.toFixed\((\d+)\)\}`',
               lambda m: f'{{fmtCurrency({m.group(1)}, {lang_var}, {m.group(2) if int(m.group(2)) != 2 else ""})}}',
               c)
    # Table cell JSX with leading $: >${x.toFixed(2)}</  (dollar then expr)
    c = re.sub(r'>\$([\w.?()\[\]'"'"' ]+)\.toFixed\((\d+)\)</',
               lambda m: f'>{{fmtCurrency({m.group(1)}, {lang_var})}}</',
               c)
    # Inline JSX dollar amounts: ${x.toFixed(2)} not inside a backtick
    c = re.sub(r'(?<![`])\$\{([\w.?()\[\]'"'"' ]+)\.toFixed\((\d+)\)\}(?![`])',
               lambda m: f'{{fmtCurrency({m.group(1)}, {lang_var})}}',
               c)
    return c

/** Format amount: ؋ symbol for Pashto, AFN prefix for English */
export function fmtCurrency(amount, lang, decimals) {
  const l = lang || 'ps';
  const d = decimals ?? 2;
  const n = Number(amount);
  if (amount == null || isNaN(n)) return l === 'ps' ? `؋0.${'0'.repeat(d)}` : `AFN 0.${'0'.repeat(d)}`;
  const formatted = n.toLocaleString('en', { minimumFractionDigits: d, maximumFractionDigits: d });
  return l === 'ps' ? `؋${formatted}` : `AFN ${formatted}`;
}
/** @deprecated use fmtCurrency(amount, lang) */
export function fmtAFN(amount, decimals) {
  return fmtCurrency(amount, 'ps', decimals);
}
/** Get currency symbol for current language */
export function currencySymbol(lang) {
  return lang === 'ps' ? '؋' : 'AFN';
}

pages = []

]

    # Replace const {t} = useI18n() OR const {t, ...} = useI18n() to include lang

               c, count=1)
    with open(fpath, 'w') as f: f.write(c)
    print(f"lang added: {fpath.split('src/pages/')[-1]}")

python3 - << 'PYEOF'
import os, re

safe_patterns = [
    'fmtCurrency', '//', 'padStart', 'generateId', 'TXN-', 'PUR-', 'EXP-',
    'CPAY-', 'className', 'toFixed(1)', 'users[0]', "t('signIn')",
    'import ', 'L`', '%`',  # liters/percent template literals are fine
]

for root, dirs, files in os.walk('/workspace/app-bqosbzxnngu9/src/pages'):
    for fname in sorted(files):
        if not fname.endswith('.jsx'): continue
        fpath = os.path.join(root, fname)
        with open(fpath) as f: lines = f.readlines()
        for i, line in enumerate(lines, 1):
            # Look for dollar sign followed by number expression
            if re.search(r'>\$\{|`\$\$\{|؋\{|>\s*؋[^<]', line):
                if not any(p in line for p in safe_patterns):
                    print(f"{fpath.split('src/pages/')[-1]}:{i}: {line.rstrip()}")
PYEOF
</action>

import os, re

for root, dirs, files in os.walk('/workspace/app-bqosbzxnngu9/src/pages'):
    for fname in sorted(files):
        if not fname.endswith('.jsx'): continue
        fpath = os.path.join(root, fname)
        with open(fpath) as f: lines = f.readlines()
        for i, line in enumerate(lines, 1):
            if '.toFixed' in line and 'fmtCurrency' not in line and '//' not in line:
                # skip percentage and liters
                if re.search(r'toFixed\(1\).*%|toFixed\(\d+\)[^)]*L[^a-z]|import|className', line):
                    continue

COMMAND:
# Fix the trailing comma in fmtCurrency calls that the regex introduced: fmtCurrency(x, lang, )
python3 - << 'PYEOF'
import os, re

for root, dirs, files in os.walk('/workspace/app-bqosbzxnngu9/src/pages'):
    for fname in sorted(files):
        if not fname.endswith('.jsx'): continue
        fpath = os.path.join(root, fname)
        with open(fpath) as f: c = f.read()
        # Fix fmtCurrency(x, lang, ) → fmtCurrency(x, lang)
        fixed = re.sub(r'fmtCurrency\(([^)]+),\s*\)', 
                       lambda m: f"fmtCurrency({m.group(1).rstrip(', ')})", c)
        if fixed != c:
            with open(fpath, 'w') as f: f.write(fixed)
            print(f"Trailing comma fixed: {fname}")

print("Done")
PYEOF
</action>

In a JSX ternary, the true branch should just be `fmtCurrency(c.creditLimit, lang)` not `{fmtCurrency(...)}`. import re

fpath = '/workspace/app-bqosbzxnngu9/src/pages/CustomersPage.jsx'
with open(fpath) as f: c = f.read()

# Fix: ternary branches must not wrap function calls in extra {}
# Pattern: ? {fmtCurrency(...)}  →  ? fmtCurrency(...)
c = re.sub(r'\?\s*\{(fmtCurrency\([^}]+\))\}', r'? \1', c)
# Also fix: : {fmtCurrency(...)}  →  : fmtCurrency(...)
c = re.sub(r':\s*\{(fmtCurrency\([^}]+\))\}', r': \1', c)

with open(fpath, 'w') as f: f.write(c)

/**
 * API service layer — mirrors the original axiosClient API surface.
 * All functions return Promises; internally uses the in-memory db store.
 */

import { db, getAll, getById, getWhere, create, update, patch, remove } from './db';

// ── Auth ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
export const authApi = {
  login: (email, password) => getWhere('users', (u) => u.email === email && u.password === password),
  findByEmail: (email) => getWhere('users', (u) => u.email === email),
  resetPassword: (id, password) => patch('users', id, { password }),
};

// ── Fuel Types ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
export const fuelTypesApi = {
  getAll: () => getAll('fuelTypes'),
  getById: (id) => getById('fuelTypes', id),
  create: (data) => create('fuelTypes', data),
  update: (id, data) => update('fuelTypes', id, data),
  delete: (id) => remove('fuelTypes', id),
};

// ── Tanks ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
export const tanksApi = {
  getAll: () => getAll('tanks'),
  getById: (id) => getById('tanks', id),
  create: (data) => create('tanks', data),
  update: (id, data) => update('tanks', id, data),
  patch: (id, data) => patch('tanks', id, data),
  delete: (id) => remove('tanks', id),
};

// ── Employees ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
export const employeesApi = {
  getAll: () => getAll('employees'),
  getById: (id) => getById('employees', id),

/**
 * In-memory database initialized from local JSON data files.
 * All mutations operate on this store; changes persist for the session.
 */

import usersData from '@/data/users.json';
import fuelTypesData from '@/data/fuelTypes.json';
import tanksData from '@/data/tanks.json';
import employeesData from '@/data/employees.json';
import customersData from '@/data/customers.json';
import fuelPricesData from '@/data/fuelPrices.json';
import purchasesData from '@/data/purchases.json';
import salesData from '@/data/sales.json';
import expensesData from '@/data/expenses.json';
import lossesData from '@/data/losses.json';
import cashHandoversData from '@/data/cashHandovers.json';
import cashStoragesData from '@/data/cashStorages.json';
import supplierPaymentsData from '@/data/supplierPayments.json';
import customerPaymentsData from '@/data/customerPayments.json';

// Deep-clone seed data so JSON imports stay immutable
const clone = (data) => JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(data));

export const db = {
  users: clone(usersData),
  fuelTypes: clone(fuelTypesData),
  tanks: clone(tanksData),
  employees: clone(employeesData),
  customers: clone(customersData),
  fuelPrices: clone(fuelPricesData),
  purchases: clone(purchasesData),
  sales: clone(salesData),
  expenses: clone(expensesData),
  losses: clone(lossesData),
  cashHandovers: clone(cashHandoversData),
  cashStorages: clone(cashStoragesData),
  supplierPayments: clone(supplierPaymentsData),
  customerPayments: clone(customerPaymentsData),
};

/** Generate a simple incremental id within a collection */
export function nextId(collection) {
  if (collection.length === 0) return '1';
  const maxId = Math.max(...collection.map((item) => parseInt(item.id, 10) || 0));
  return String(maxId + 1);
}

/** Simulate async latency (feel like real API) */
const delay = (ms = 50) => new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms));

#!/bin/bash

VITE_TEMP="node_modules/.vite-temp"
if [ -L "$VITE_TEMP" ]; then
    rm "$VITE_TEMP"
    mkdir -p "$VITE_TEMP"
elif [ ! -e "$VITE_TEMP" ]; then
    mkdir -p "$VITE_TEMP"
fi

OUTPUT=$(npx vite build --minify false --logLevel error --outDir /workspace/.dist 2>&1)
EXIT_CODE=$?

if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
    echo "$OUTPUT"
fi

exit $EXIT_CODE

<action>
AgentThinkAction(thought='The vite.config.dev.js uses `__dirname` but never defines it. In ES modules (type: "module" in package.json), `__dirname` is not available. But vite.config.dev.js loads the userConfig from vite.config.js via `loadConfigFromFile`, which does define __dirname. However, the vite.config.dev.js itself uses __dirname on lines 17 and 35 without defining it.\n\nLooking at line 17: `const configFile = path.resolve(__dirname, "vite.config.js");` - this is inside the `defineConfig(async () => {` callback. The `__dirname` here refers to the vite.config.dev.js directory.\n\nBut wait - vite itself might be handling this... Let me check. Actually, Vite processes config files specially - it might handle the `__dirname` for config files. But since package.json has `"type": "module"`, Node.js treats all .js files as ESM. However, Vite\'s `defineConfig` file loading might transpile/bundle the config file before executing it.\n\nActually, when Vite loads the config file, it bundles it with esbuild first, which defines `__dirname` for the bundled output. So this should actually work when Vite loads it.\n\nThe real question is: why is the preview not starting? Let me think about what other issues might exist.\n\nThe platform probably starts the dev server by running `npx vite --config vite.config.dev.js`. This works fine as we tested it. \n\nMaybe the issue is that a previous vite process is still using port 5173, or there\'s some other startup issue. Let me check if there\'s any port conflict or if we need to do something else to trigger a platform restart.', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)
</action>

    import * as vite from 'vite';
    import { defineConfig, loadConfigFromFile } from "vite";

      makeTagger,

    export default defineConfig(async () => {
      const env: ConfigEnv = { command: "serve", mode: "development" };
      const configFile = path.resolve(__dirname, "vite.config.ts");
      const result = await loadConfigFromFile(env, configFile);
      const userConfig = result?.config;

      const viteVersionInfo = {
        version: vite.version,
        rollupVersion: (vite as any).rollupVersion ?? null,
        rolldownVersion: (vite as any).rolldownVersion ?? null,
        isRolldownVite: 'rolldownVersion' in vite
      };

      return {
        ...userConfig,
        define: {
          __VITE_INFO__: JSON.stringify(viteVersionInfo),
          ...(userConfig?.define || {})
        },
        // 将 Vite 缓存目录设置为项目本地目录，避免在 /workspace/node_modules/ 下创建
        cacheDir: path.resolve(__dirname, "node_modules/.vite"),
        server: {
          ...(userConfig?.server || {}),
          warmup: {}
        },
        plugins: [
          makeTagger(),
          injectedGuiListenerPlugin({
            path: 'https://miaoda-resource-static.s3cdn.medo.dev/common/v2/injected.js'
          }),
          injectOnErrorPlugin(),
          ...(userConfig?.plugins || []),
          
{
  name: 'hmr-toggle',
  configureServer(server) {
    let hmrEnabled = true;

    // 包装原来的 send 方法
    const _send = server.ws.send;
    server.ws.send = (payload) => {
      if (hmrEnabled) {
        return _send.call(server.ws, payload);
      } else {
        console.log('[HMR disabled] skipped payload:', payload.type);
      }
    };

    // 提供接口切换 HMR
    server.middlewares.use('/innerapi/v1/sourcecode/__hmr_off', (req, res) => {
      hmrEnabled = false;
      let body = {
          status: 0,
          msg: 'HMR disabled'
      };
      res.setHeader('Content-Type', 'application/json');
      res.end(JSON.stringify(body));
    });

    server.middlewares.use('/innerapi/v1/sourcecode/__hmr_on', (req, res) => {
      hmrEnabled = true;
      let body = {
          status: 0,
          msg: 'HMR enabled'
      };
      res.setHeader('Content-Type', 'application/json');
      res.end(JSON.stringify(body));
    });

    // 注册一个 HTTP API，用来手动触发一次整体刷新
    server.middlewares.use('/innerapi/v1/sourcecode/__hmr_reload', (req, res) => {
      if (hmrEnabled) {
        server.ws.send({
          type: 'full-reload',
          path: '*', // 整页刷新
        });
      }
      res.statusCode = 200;
      let body = {
          status: 0,
          msg: 'Manual full reload triggered'
      };
      res.setHeader('Content-Type', 'application/json');
      res.end(JSON.stringify(body));
    });
  },
  load(id) {
    if (id === 'virtual:after-update') {
      return `
        if (import.meta.hot) {
          import.meta.hot.on('vite:afterUpdate', () => {
            window.postMessage(
              {
                type: 'editor-update'
              },
              '*'
            );
          });
        }
      `;
    }
  },
  transformIndexHtml(html) {
    return {
      html,
      tags: [
        {
          tag: 'script',
          attrs: {
            type: 'module',
            src: '/@id/virtual:after-update'
          },
          injectTo: 'body'
        }
      ]
    };
  }
},

<action>
**MessageAction** (source=EventSource.AGENT)
CONTENT: Zero errors. Here's what was fixed:

**Reports table not updating:**
The root cause was index-based `key={i}` on `<tbody>` and `<tr>` rows. When switching between Daily / Weekly / Monthly (all sharing the same switch-case columns), React reused existing DOM nodes and skipped re-rendering cell content even though the data changed. Fixed by adding a composite `key={reportType}-${dateFrom}-${dateTo}` to the `<tbody>` and each `<tr>`, forcing a full DOM remount whenever the report type or date range changes.

**Cash Storage — AFN currency:**
- All 4 seed records updated from `"currency": "USD"` → `"currency": "AFN"`
- Form default values changed from `'USD'` → `'AFN'`
- `'AFN'` added as the first option in the currency selector dropdown
</action>

    69	  });
    70	
    71	  const invalidate = () => qc.invalidateQueries({queryKey: ['cashStorages']});
    72	
    73	  const generateId = () => `STR-${String(storages.length + 1).padStart(3, '0')}`;
    74	
    75	  const createMutation = useMutation({mutationFn: (d) => cashStoragesApi.create(d),
    76	    onSuccess: () => {
    77	      toast.success(t('storageAdded'));
    78	      invalidate();
    79	      setDialog({ open: false});
    80	    },
    81	    onError: () => toast.error(t('failedCreate')),
    82	  });
    83	  const updateMutation = useMutation({mutationFn: ({ id, data}) =>
    84	      cashStoragesApi.update(id, data),
    85	    onSuccess: () => {toast.success(t('storageUpdated'));
    86	      invalidate();
    87	      setDialog({ open: false});
    88	    },
    89	    onError: () => toast.error(t('failedUpdate')),
    90	  });
    91	  const deleteMutation = useMutation({mutationFn: (id) => cashStoragesApi.delete(id),
    92	    onSuccess: () => {
    93	      toast.success(t('deleteSuccess'));
    94	      invalidate();
    95	      setDeleteId(null);},
    96	    onError: () => toast.error(t('failedDelete')),
    97	  });
    98	
    99	  const openCreate = () => {form.reset({ name: '', type: 'Office Safe', balance: 0, currency: 'AFN', notes: ''});
   100	    setDialog({open: true});
   101	  };
   102	  const openEdit = (item) => {form.reset({
   103	      name: item.name,
   104	      type: item.StorageType,
   105	      balance: item.balance,
   106	      currency: item.currency,
   107	      notes: item.notes});
   108	    setDialog({open: true, item});
   109	  };
   110	
   111	  const onSubmit = (values) => {
   112	    values.amount = toArabicNum(values.amount);const data = {
   113	      ...values,
   114	      storageId: dialog.item?.storageId ?? generateId(),
   115	      notes: values.notes ?? '',
   116	      lastUpdated: format(new Date(), 'yyyy-MM-dd')};
   117	    if (dialog.item) updateMutation.mutate({id: dialog.item.id, data});
   118	    else createMutation.mutate(data);
   119	  };
   120	
   121	  const totalBalance = storages.reduce((a, s) => a + s.balance, 0);
   122	
   123	  return (
   124	    <AppLayout title={t('cashStorageTitle')}>
   125	      <div className="space-y-6">
   126	        {/* Summary cards */}
   127	        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4 md:grid-cols-4">
   128	          {storages.map((s) => (
   129	            <Card key={s.id} className="h-full">
   130	              <CardContent className="p-4">
   131	                <div className="flex items-start justify-between">
   132	                  <div className="min-w-0">
   133	                    <p className="truncate text-xs text-muted-foreground">{s.name}</p>
   134	                    <p className="mt-1 text-lg font-bold text-foreground">
   135	                      {fmtCurrency(s.balance, lang)}
   136	                    </p>
   137	                    <p className="mt-0.5 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
   138	                      {s.currency} • {s.type}
   139	                    </p>
   140	                  </div>
   141	                  <span className="text-2xl">{typeIcons[s.type] ?? '💰'}</span>
   142	                </div>
   143	              </CardContent>
   144	            </Card>
   145	          ))}
   146	        </div>
   147	
   148	        {storages.length > 0 && (
   149	          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 rounded-lg border border-primary/20 bg-primary/10 p-3">
   150	            <FiCreditCard className="h-4 w-4 shrink-0 text-primary" />
   151	            <p className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground">
   152	              Total Cash Holdings:{' '}
   153	              <span className="font-bold text-primary">{fmtCurrency(totalBalance, lang)}</span>
   154	            </p>
   155	          </div>
   156	        )}
   157	
   158	        {/* Table */}
   159	        <Card>
   160	          <CardHeader>
[The command completed with exit code 0.]
[Current working directory: /workspace]
--END AGENT OBSERVATION--
</observation>
<action>
**CmdRunAction (source=EventSource.AGENT, is_input=False)**

cat -n /workspace/app-bqosbzxnngu9/src/components/layouts/AppLayout.jsx
</action>

  "py_interpreter_path": null,
  "prefix": "",
  "suffix": "\n[The command completed with exit code 0.]"

    81	// ─── Language selector dropdown ───────────────────────────────────────────────
    82	function LangSelector({ compact = false }) {
    83	  const { lang, switchLang, t } = useI18n();
    84	  return (
    85	    <DropdownMenu>
    86	      <DropdownMenuTrigger asChild>
    87	        <Button
    88	          variant="ghost"
    89	          size="sm"
    90	          className={clsx(
    91	            'text-sidebar-foreground hover:bg-sidebar-accent hover:text-sidebar-accent-foreground',
    92	            compact ? 'w-9 px-0' : 'flex-1'
    93	          )}
    94	          title={t('language')}
    95	        >
    96	          <FiGlobe className="h-4 w-4 shrink-0" />
    97	          {!compact && (
    98	            <span className="ms-2 text-xs">{lang === 'ps' ? 'پښتو' : 'EN'}</span>
    99	          )}
   100	        </Button>
   101	      </DropdownMenuTrigger>
   102	      <DropdownMenuContent align="end" className="min-w-[120px]">
   103	        <DropdownMenuItem
   104	          onClick={() => switchLang('ps')}
   105	          className={clsx('gap-2 font-medium', lang === 'ps' && 'text-primary')}
   106	        >
   107	          <span className="text-base leading-none">🇦🇫</span>
   108	          {t('pashto')}
   109	          {lang === 'ps' && <span className="ms-auto text-primary">✓</span>}
   110	        </DropdownMenuItem>
   111	        <DropdownMenuItem
   112	          onClick={() => switchLang('en')}
   113	          className={clsx('gap-2 font-medium', lang === 'en' && 'text-primary')}
   114	        >
   115	          <span className="text-base leading-none">🇬🇧</span>
   116	          {t('english')}
   117	          {lang === 'en' && <span className="ms-auto text-primary">✓</span>}
   118	        </DropdownMenuItem>
   119	      </DropdownMenuContent>
   120	    </DropdownMenu>
   121	  );
   122	}

   124	// ─── Sidebar navigation ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   125	function SidebarNav({ onClose }) {
   126	  const location = useLocation();
   127	  const { user } = useAppSelector((s) => s.auth);
   128	  const navItems = useNavItems();
   129	
   130	  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(() => {
   131	    // Keep parent groups open by default
   132	    return navItems
   133	      .filter((i) => i.children)
   134	      .map((i) => i.labelKey);
   135	  });
   136	
   137	  const toggle = (key) =>
   138	    setExpanded((prev) =>
   139	      prev.includes(key) ? prev.filter((l) => l !== key) : [...prev, key]
   140	    );
   141	
   142	  const isActive      = (path) => path === location.pathname;
   143	  const isParentActive = (item) =>
   144	    item.children?.some((c) => c.path === location.pathname) ?? false;
   145	  const allowed = (item) => !item.roles || item.roles.includes(user?.role ?? '');
   146	
   147	  return (
   148	    <nav className="flex flex-col gap-1 p-3">
   149	      {navItems.filter(allowed).map((item) => {
   150	        if (item.children) {
   151	          const isOpen = expanded.includes(item.labelKey);
   152	          const parentActive = isParentActive(item);
   153	          return (
   154	            <div key={item.labelKey}>
   155	              <button
   156	                onClick={() => toggle(item.labelKey)}
   157	                className={clsx(
   158	                  'flex w-full items-center gap-3 rounded-lg px-3 py-2.5 text-left text-sm font-medium transition-colors',
   159	                  parentActive
   160	                    ? 'bg-sidebar-accent text-sidebar-primary'
   161	                    : 'text-sidebar-foreground hover:bg-sidebar-accent hover:text-sidebar-accent-foreground'
   162	                )}
   163	              >
   164	                <item.icon className="h-4 w-4 shrink-0" />
   165	                <span className="min-w-0 flex-1 truncate">{item.label}</span>
   166	                {isOpen ? (
   167	                  <FiChevronDown className="h-3 w-3 shrink-0" />
   168	                ) : (
   169	                  <FiChevronRight className="h-3 w-3 shrink-0" />
   170	                )}
   171	              </button>
   172	              {isOpen && (
   173	                <div className="ms-7 mt-1 flex flex-col gap-1">
   174	                  {item.children.map((child) => (
   175	                    <Link
   176	                      key={child.path}
   177	                      to={child.path}
   178	                      onClick={onClose}
   179	                      className={clsx(
   180	                        'rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-sm transition-colors',
   181	                        isActive(child.path)
   182	                          ? 'bg-sidebar-primary font-medium text-sidebar-primary-foreground'
   183	                          : 'text-sidebar-foreground hover:bg-sidebar-accent hover:text-sidebar-accent-foreground'
   184	                      )}
   185	                    >
   186	                      {child.label}
   187	                    </Link>
   188	                  ))}
   189	                </div>
   190	              )}
   191	            </div>
   192	          );
   193	        }
   194	        return (
   195	          <Link
   196	            key={item.path}
   197	            to={item.path ?? ''}
   198	            onClick={onClose}
   199	            className={clsx(
   200	              'flex items-center gap-3 rounded-lg px-3 py-2.5 text-sm font-medium transition-colors',
   201	              isActive(item.path)
   202	                ? 'bg-sidebar-primary text-sidebar-primary-foreground'
   203	                : 'text-sidebar-foreground hover:bg-sidebar-accent hover:text-sidebar-accent-foreground'
   204	            )}
   205	          >
   206	            <item.icon className="h-4 w-4 shrink-0" />
   207	            <span className="min-w-0 truncate">{item.label}</span>
   208	          </Link>
   209	        );
   210	      })}
   211	    </nav>
   212	  );
   213	}

   215	// ─── Main layout ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   216	export default function AppLayout({ children, title }) {
   217	  const [mobileOpen, setMobileOpen] = useState(false);
   218	  const [darkMode, setDarkMode] = useState(() =>
   219	    document.documentElement.classList.contains('dark')
   220	  );
   221	  const { user }   = useAppSelector((s) => s.auth);
   222	  const { t }      = useI18n();
   223	  const dispatch   = useAppDispatch();
   224	  const navigate   = useNavigate();
   225	
   226	  const handleLogout = () => {
   227	    dispatch(logout());
   228	    navigate('/login');
   229	  };
   230	
   231	  const toggleDark = () => {
   232	    const isDark = document.documentElement.classList.toggle('dark');
   233	    setDarkMode(isDark);
   234	  };
   235	
   236	  const roleBadgeColor = {
   237	    admin:    'bg-primary text-primary-foreground',
   238	    manager:  'bg-yellow-500/20 text-yellow-700 dark:text-yellow-400',
   239	    operator: 'bg-blue-500/20 text-blue-700 dark:text-blue-400',
   240	  }[user?.role ?? 'operator'];
   241	
   242	  // ── Shared bottom-bar buttons ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   243	  const BottomBar = () => (
   244	    <div className="flex gap-1 border-t border-sidebar-border p-3">
   245	      {/* Dark/Light */}
   246	      <Button
   247	        variant="ghost"
   248	        size="sm"
   249	        onClick={toggleDark}
   250	        className="flex-1 text-sidebar-foreground hover:bg-sidebar-accent hover:text-sidebar-accent-foreground"
   251	      >
   252	        {darkMode ? <FiSun className="h-4 w-4" /> : <FiMoon className="h-4 w-4" />}
   253	        <span className="ms-1.5 text-xs">{darkMode ? t('lightMode') : t('darkMode')}</span>
   254	      </Button>
   255	
   256	      {/* Language */}
   257	      <LangSelector />
   258	
   259	      {/* Logout */}
   260	      <Button
   261	        variant="ghost"
   262	        size="sm"
   263	        onClick={handleLogout}
   264	        className="flex-1 text-sidebar-foreground hover:bg-sidebar-accent hover:text-sidebar-accent-foreground"
   265	      >
   266	        <FiLogOut className="h-4 w-4" />
   267	        <span className="ms-1.5 text-xs">{t('logout')}</span>
   268	      </Button>
   269	    </div>
   270	  );
   271	
   272	  return (
   273	    <div className="flex h-screen w-full overflow-hidden bg-background">
   274	      {/* ── Desktop sidebar ─────────────────────────────────────────────────── */}
   275	      <aside className="hidden h-screen w-64 shrink-0 flex-col border-e border-sidebar-border bg-sidebar lg:flex">
   276	        {/* Logo */}
   277	        <div className="flex items-center gap-3 border-b border-sidebar-border px-4 py-4">
   278	          <div className="flex h-9 w-9 shrink-0 items-center justify-center rounded-lg bg-sidebar-primary">
   279	            <FiActivity className="h-5 w-5 text-sidebar-primary-foreground" />
   280	          </div>
   281	          <div className="min-w-0">
   282	            <p className="truncate text-sm font-bold text-sidebar-foreground">{t('appName')}</p>
   283	            <p className="truncate text-xs text-sidebar-foreground/60">{t('appSubtitle')}</p>
   284	          </div>
   285	        </div>
   286	
   287	        {/* User badge */}
   288	        <div className="border-b border-sidebar-border px-4 py-3">
   289	          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
   290	            <div className="flex h-8 w-8 shrink-0 items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-sidebar-accent">
   291	              <span className="text-sm font-semibold text-sidebar-foreground">
   292	                {user?.name?.charAt(0).toUpperCase()}
   293	              </span>
   294	            </div>
   295	            <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
   296	              <p className="truncate text-sm font-medium text-sidebar-foreground">{user?.name}</p>
   297	              <span className={clsx('rounded-full px-2 py-0.5 text-xs font-medium capitalize', roleBadgeColor)}>
   298	                {user?.role}
   299	              </span>
   300	            </div>
   301	          </div>
   302	        </div>
   303	
   304	        {/* Nav */}
   305	        <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto scroll-smooth">
   306	          <SidebarNav />
   307	        </div>
   308	
   309	        <BottomBar />
   310	      </aside>
   311	
   312	      {/* ── Mobile sidebar overlay ─────────────────────────────────────────── */}
   313	      {mobileOpen && (
   314	        <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 lg:hidden">
   315	          <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-black/50" onClick={() => setMobileOpen(false)} />
   316	          <aside className="absolute start-0 top-0 flex h-full w-72 flex-col overflow-y-auto scroll-smooth bg-sidebar">
   317	            <div className="flex items-center justify-between border-b border-sidebar-border px-4 py-4">
   318	              <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
   319	                <FiActivity className="h-5 w-5 text-sidebar-primary" />
   320	                <span className="text-sm font-bold text-sidebar-foreground">{t('appName')}</span>
   321	              </div>
   322	              <button onClick={() => setMobileOpen(false)} className="text-sidebar-foreground">
   323	                <FiX className="h-5 w-5" />
   324	              </button>
   325	            </div>
   326	            <div className="border-b border-sidebar-border px-4 py-3">
   327	              <p className="text-sm font-medium text-sidebar-foreground">{user?.name}</p>
   328	              <span className={clsx('rounded-full px-2 py-0.5 text-xs font-medium capitalize', roleBadgeColor)}>
   329	                {user?.role}
   330	              </span>
   331	            </div>
   332	            <div className="flex-1">
   333	              <SidebarNav onClose={() => setMobileOpen(false)} />
   334	            </div>
   335	            <BottomBar />
   336	          </aside>
   337	        </div>
   338	      )}
   339	
   340	      {/* ── Main content ────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */}
   341	      <div className="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col overflow-x-hidden h-screen">
   342	        {/* Top header */}

   344	          {/* Mobile hamburger */}
   345	          <button
   346	            className="rounded-md p-1.5 transition-colors hover:bg-muted lg:hidden"
   347	            onClick={() => setMobileOpen(true)}
   348	          >
   349	            <FiMenu className="h-5 w-5" />
   350	          </button>
   351	
   352	          {/* Page title */}
   353	          <h1 className="min-w-0 flex-1 truncate text-balance text-base font-semibold text-foreground">
   354	            {title}
   355	          </h1>
   356	
   357	          {/* Header actions */}
   358	          <div className="flex shrink-0 items-center gap-1">
   359	            {/* Language selector (header – desktop) */}
   360	            <div className="hidden lg:flex">
   361	              <HeaderLangSelector />
   362	            </div>
   363	
   364	            {/* Notification bell */}
   365	            <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" className="relative p-2">
   366	              <FiBell className="h-4 w-4" />
   367	              <Badge className="absolute -end-1 -top-1 flex h-4 w-4 items-center justify-center bg-destructive p-0 text-xs text-destructive-foreground">
   368	                3
   369	              </Badge>
   370	            </Button>
   371	          </div>
   372	        </header>
   373	
   374	        {/* Page body */}
   375	        <main className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto scroll-smooth p-4 md:p-6">{children}</main>
   376	      </div>
   377	    </div>
   378	  );

   409	  return (

    </div>
  )}

  {/* ── Main content ────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */}
  <div className="flex min-w-0 flex-1 flex-col overflow-x-hidden h-screen">
    {/* Top header */}
    <header className="flex h-14 shrink-0 items-center gap-3 border-b border-border bg-card px-4">
      {/* Mobile hamburger */}
      <button
        className="rounded-md p-1.5 transition-colors hover:bg-muted lg:hidden"
        onClick={() => setMobileOpen(true)}
      >
        <FiMenu className="h-5 w-5" />
      </button>

      {/* Page title */}
      <h1 className="min-w-0 flex-1 truncate text-balance text-base font-semibold text-foreground">
        {title}
      </h1>

      {/* Header actions */}
      <div className="flex shrink-0 items-center gap-1">
        {/* Notification bell */}
        <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" className="relative p-2">
          <FiBell className="h-4 w-4" />
          <Badge className="absolute -end-1 -top-1 flex h-4 w-4 items-center justify-center bg-destructive p-0 text-xs text-destructive-foreground">
            3
          </Badge>
        </Button>

        {/* Language selector */}
        <DropdownMenu>
          <DropdownMenuTrigger asChild>
            <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" className="gap-1.5 px-2 text-foreground hover:bg-muted" title={t('language')}>
              <FiGlobe className="h-4 w-4" />
              <span className="hidden text-xs font-medium md:inline">{lang === 'ps' ? 'پښتو' : 'EN'}</span>
              <FiChevronDown className="hidden h-3 w-3 md:inline" />
            </Button>
          </DropdownMenuTrigger>
          <DropdownMenuContent align="end" className="min-w-[130px]">
            <DropdownMenuItem
              onClick={() => switchLang('ps')}
              className={clsx('gap-2 font-medium', lang === 'ps' && 'text-primary')}
            >
              <span className="text-base leading-none">🇦🇫</span>
              {t('pashto')}
              {lang === 'ps' && <span className="ms-auto text-primary">✓</span>}
            </DropdownMenuItem>
            <DropdownMenuItem
              onClick={() => switchLang('en')}
              className={clsx('gap-2 font-medium', lang === 'en' && 'text-primary')}
            >
              <span className="text-base leading-none">🇬🇧</span>
              {t('english')}
              {lang === 'en' && <span className="ms-auto text-primary">✓</span>}
            </DropdownMenuItem>
          </DropdownMenuContent>
        </DropdownMenu>

        {/* Dark / Light toggle */}
        <Button
          variant="ghost"
          size="sm"
          onClick={toggleDark}
          className="p-2 text-foreground hover:bg-muted"
          title={darkMode ? t('lightMode') : t('darkMode')}
        >
          {darkMode ? <FiSun className="h-4 w-4" /> : <FiMoon className="h-4 w-4" />}
        </Button>

        {/* Avatar + logout dropdown */}
        <DropdownMenu>
          <DropdownMenuTrigger asChild>
            <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" className="gap-2 px-2 text-foreground hover:bg-muted">
              <div className="flex h-7 w-7 shrink-0 items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-primary text-primary-foreground text-xs font-bold">
                {user?.name?.charAt(0).toUpperCase()}
              </div>
              <div className="hidden text-left md:block">
                <p className="max-w-[100px] truncate text-xs font-medium leading-none">{user?.name}</p>
                <span className={clsx('mt-0.5 inline-block rounded-full px-1.5 py-px text-[10px] font-medium capitalize', roleBadgeColor)}>
                  {user?.role}
                </span>
              </div>
              <FiChevronDown className="hidden h-3 w-3 shrink-0 md:block" />
            </Button>
          </DropdownMenuTrigger>
          <DropdownMenuContent align="end" className="w-44">
            <div className="px-2 py-1.5">
              <p className="truncate text-sm font-medium text-foreground">{user?.name}</p>
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground capitalize">{user?.role}</p>
            </div>
            <div className="my-1 border-t border-border" />
            <DropdownMenuItem
              onClick={handleLogout}
              className="gap-2 text-destructive focus:text-destructive"
            >
              <FiLogOut className="h-4 w-4" />
              {t('logout')}
            </DropdownMenuItem>
          </DropdownMenuContent>
        </DropdownMenu>
      </div>
    </header>

    {/* Page body */}
    <main className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto scroll-smooth p-4 md:p-6">{children}</main>
  </div>
</div>
); }
